GT T-independent: 28.58*ε^2 - 1205.7*ε^3 + 80.56

From T-dependent: need 3c0*c1 = 0 (no T*ε^2), 3c0*c1^2 = 0 (no T*ε). So c1=0.
Then T-independent has no ε^3 term. Cannot match.
Candidate 14 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 15:** `T*c0*(c1+ε)^3 + c2*ε^2 + c3*log(T*c4+1) + c5*ε + c6`
log(T*c4+1) ≠ T. Cannot match.
